msg = '', tolerance = 0.02

    def assert_dict_equal(actual, expected, msg="", tolerance=0.02):
        """Assert dicts are equal using deepdiff for better error messages.
    
        Args:
            actual: The actual result dict
            expected: The expected result dict
            msg: Optional message for assertion failure
            tolerance: Tolerance for numeric comparisons (default 0.02)
        """
        diff = DeepDiff(
            actual,
            expected,
            ignore_order=True,
            math_epsilon=tolerance,
            ignore_numeric_type_changes=True,
        )

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        "case_name,invention_skill",
        FUNCTIONALITY_CASES,
    )
    def test_functionality(
        case_name, invention_skill, entrypoint_argv, sde_dir, tmp_path
    ):
        """Functionality: Extended functionality tests."""
        expected_materials = load_csv_materials(4, case_name)
        expected_jobs = load_csv_jobs(4, case_name)
    
        config_path = create_config_file(
            checkpoint=4,
            path=tmp_path,
            te_bonus=20,
            invention_skill=invention_skill,
        )
        output_dir = tmp_path / "outputs"
        output_dir.mkdir()
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv,
            "plan",
            load_build_string(4, case_name).strip(),
            "--sde",
            str(sde_dir),
            "--config",
            str(config_path),
            "--output",
            str(output_dir),
        )
        assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        "case_name,invention_skill",
        FUNCTIONALITY_CASES,
    )
    def test_functionality(
        case_name, invention_skill, entrypoint_argv, sde_dir, tmp_path
    ):
        """Functionality: Extended functionality tests."""
        expected_materials = load_csv_materials(4, case_name)
        expected_jobs = load_csv_jobs(4, case_name)
    
        config_path = create_config_file(
            checkpoint=4,
            path=tmp_path,
            te_bonus=20,
            invention_skill=invention_skill,
        )
        output_dir = tmp_path / "outputs"
        output_dir.mkdir()
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv,
            "plan",
            load_build_string(4, case_name).strip(),
            "--sde",
            str(sde_dir),
            "--config",
            str(config_path),
            "--output",
            str(output_dir),
        )
        assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"
    
        actual_materials = parse_output_csv(output_dir / "materials.csv")
        actual_jobs = parse_output_csv(output_dir / "jobs.csv")

case_name = 'barrage_l_30d', split_days = 30, timeout = 60
entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'industry.py']
sde_dir = PosixPath('/workspace/.evaluation_tests/assets/sde_dir')
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_build_all_core_barrage_l_0')

    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        "case_name,split_days,timeout", CORE_CASES, ids=[c[0] for c in CORE_CASES]
    )
    def test_build_all_core(
        case_name,
        split_days,
        timeout,
        entrypoint_argv,
        sde_dir,
        tmp_path,
    ):
        """Core: Build-all with job splitting."""
        # Load expected data from CSV files
        expected_jobs = load_csv_jobs(5, case_name)
        expected_materials = load_csv_materials(5, case_name)
        build_string = load_build_string(5, case_name).strip()
    
        # Create config and run command
        config_path = create_config_file(
            checkpoint=5,
            path=tmp_path,
            te_bonus=20,
            invention_skill=3,
            split_days=split_days,
            component_me=10,
            component_te=20,
        )
        output_dir = tmp_path / "outputs"
        output_dir.mkdir()
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv,
            "plan",
            build_string,
            "--sde",
            str(sde_dir),
            "--build-all",
            "--config",
            str(config_path),
            "--output",
            str(output_dir),
            timeout=timeout,
        )
        assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"
    
        # Parse and normalize actual output
        actual_jobs = normalize_csv_jobs(parse_csv_file(output_dir / "jobs.csv"))
        actual_materials = normalize_csv_materials(
            parse_csv_file(output_dir / "materials.csv")

    @pytest.mark.parametrize(

        case_name,

        entrypoint_argv,
        sde_dir,
        tmp_path,
    ):
        """Core: Build-all with job splitting."""
        # Load expected data from CSV files
        expected_jobs = load_csv_jobs(5, case_name)
        expected_materials = load_csv_materials(5, case_name)
        build_string = load_build_string(5, case_name).strip()
    
        # Create config and run command
        config_path = create_config_file(
            checkpoint=5,
            path=tmp_path,
            te_bonus=20,
            invention_skill=3,
            split_days=split_days,
            component_me=10,
            component_te=20,
        )
        output_dir = tmp_path / "outputs"
        output_dir.mkdir()
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv,
            "plan",
            build_string,
            "--sde",
            str(sde_dir),
            "--build-all",
            "--config",
            str(config_path),
            "--output",
            str(output_dir),
            timeout=timeout,
        )
        assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"
    
        # Parse and normalize actual output
        actual_jobs = normalize_csv_jobs(parse_csv_file(output_dir / "jobs.csv"))
        actual_materials = normalize_csv_materials(
            parse_csv_file(output_dir / "materials.csv")
        )

    def assert_dict_equal(actual, expected, msg="", tolerance=0.02):
        """Assert dicts are equal using deepdiff for better error messages.
    
        Args:
            actual: The actual result dict
            expected: The expected result dict
            msg: Optional message for assertion failure
            tolerance: Tolerance for numeric comparisons (default 0.02)
        """
        diff = DeepDiff(
            actual,
            expected,
            ignore_order=True,
            math_epsilon=tolerance,
            ignore_numeric_type_changes=True,
        )
